\mbox{\Hypertarget{_atmega328_p_8h_a610f14a737738abf63fbffe287cc74ad}\label{_atmega328_p_8h_a610f14a737738abf63fbffe287cc74ad}} 
\index{Atmega328P.h@{Atmega328P.h}!ClkSelect@{ClkSelect}}
\index{ClkSelect@{ClkSelect}!Atmega328P.h@{Atmega328P.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ClkSelect}{ClkSelect}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{_atmega328_p_8h_a610f14a737738abf63fbffe287cc74ad}{Clk\+Select}}}



This enumerate defines the values for 8bit and 16 bit timer counter blocks Note\+: The values prefixed with CS\+\_\+ are valid for all timer counter blocks The values prefixed with T1 are valid for Tcnt0 and Tcnt1 The values prefixed with T2 are valid for Tcnt2.
